### 4.2 琛屽姩灞傦細鎵ц寮曟搸涓庤ˉ鍋夸簨鍔?

#### 4.3.3 杩涘寲瑙﹀彂鏈哄埗

**璁板繂杩涘寲鏉′欢**锛?```python
def should_evolve(memory):
    """鍒ゆ柇璁板繂鏄惁闇€瑕佽繘鍖栧埌鏇撮珮灞傜骇"""
    
    # 鏉′欢 1: 璁块棶棰戠巼杈惧埌闃堝€?    if memory.access_count >= EVOLUTION_THRESHOLD:
        return True
    
    # 鏉′欢 2: 涓庡叾浠栬蹇嗗舰鎴愬己鍏宠仈
    if len(memory.strong_connections) >= MIN_CONNECTIONS:
        return True
    
    # 鏉′欢 3: 琚爣璁颁负閲嶈
    if memory.importance_score > IMPORTANCE_THRESHOLD:
        return True
    
    return False
```

鈹屸攢鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹?鈹?        妯″瀷鍗忓悓鏋舵瀯                      鈹?鈹溾攢鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹?鈹?                                        鈹?鈹? 涓绘ā鍨?(Primary Model)                  鈹?鈹? - GPT-4 / Claude / 鑷爺澶фā鍨?          鈹?鈹? - 鑱岃矗锛氭繁搴︽帹鐞嗐€佸鏉傝鍒?                鈹?鈹?                                        鈹?鈹? 鈫?鍗忚皟                                  鈹?鈹?                                        鈹?鈹? 杈呮ā鍨?1          杈呮ā鍨?2               鈹?鈹? - GPT-3.5        - Llama-3             鈹?鈹? - 鑱岃矗锛氬揩閫熷搷搴斻€佸父瑙勪换鍔?                鈹?鈹?                                        鈹?鈹? 鈫?浠茶                                  鈹?鈹?                                        鈹?鈹? 浠茶鍣?(Arbiter)                        鈹?鈹? - 浜ゅ弶楠岃瘉                              鈹?鈹? - 鍐茬獊瑙ｅ喅                              鈹?鈹? - 璐ㄩ噺璇勪及                              鈹?鈹?                                        鈹?鈹斺攢鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹?```

**鍥?4-5**锛氫富杈呮ā鍨嬪崗鍚屾灦鏋勫浘

#### 4.4.2 浜ゅ弶楠岃瘉鏈哄埗

**楠岃瘉绛栫暐**锛?```python
def cross_validate(primary_output, auxiliary_outputs):
    """
    浜ゅ弶楠岃瘉涓绘ā鍨嬩笌杈呮ā鍨嬬殑杈撳嚭
    
    Args:
        primary_output: 涓绘ā鍨嬭緭鍑?        auxiliary_outputs: 澶氫釜杈呮ā鍨嬭緭鍑?    
    Returns:
        validated_result: 楠岃瘉鍚庣殑缁撴灉
        confidence_score: 缃俊搴﹀垎鏁?    """
    
    # Step 1: 璇箟鐩镐技搴﹁绠?    similarities = [
        cosine_similarity(primary_output, aux_output)
        for aux_output in auxiliary_outputs
    ]
    
    # Step 2: 涓€鑷存€ф鏌?    if all(sim > CONSENSUS_THRESHOLD for sim in similarities):
        # 楂樺害涓€鑷达紝鐩存帴杩斿洖
        return primary_output, 0.95
    
    # Step 3: 鍐茬獊妫€娴嬩笌瑙ｅ喅
    conflicts = detect_conflicts(primary_output, auxiliary_outputs)
    if conflicts:
        # 鍚姩浠茶绋嬪簭
        return arbiter_resolve(conflicts), 0.70
    
    # Step 4: 鍔犳潈铻嶅悎
    return weighted_fusion(primary_output, auxiliary_outputs), 0.85
```

**浠ｇ爜娓呭崟 4-8**锛氫氦鍙夐獙璇佺畻娉?

    },
    {

**浠ｇ爜娓呭崟 4-9**锛氫徊瑁佽鍒欓厤缃?
#### 4.4.4 Token 鏁堢巼浼樺寲

**鏅鸿兘璺敱绛栫暐**锛?```python
def route_request(request):
    """
    鏍规嵁璇锋眰澶嶆潅搴︽櫤鑳借矾鐢卞埌鍚堥€傜殑妯″瀷
    
    绛栫暐锛?    - 绠€鍗曢棶棰?鈫?灏忔ā鍨嬶紙鑺傜渷 Token锛?    - 澶嶆潅鎺ㄧ悊 鈫?澶фā鍨嬶紙淇濊瘉璐ㄩ噺锛?    - 鏁忔劅鍐呭 鈫?涓绘ā鍨嬶紙鍙帶鎬у己锛?    """
    
    complexity = estimate_complexity(request)
    
    if complexity < 0.3:
        return "auxiliary_small_model"
    elif complexity < 0.7:
        return "auxiliary_medium_model"
    else:
        return "primary_large_model"
```

### 9.2 Go SDK

#### 9.2.1 瀹夎

```bash
go get github.com/spharx/agentos-sdk-go
```

#### 9.2.2 蹇€熷紑濮?
```go
package main

import (
    "context"
    "fmt"
    agentos "github.com/spharx/agentos-sdk-go"
)

func main() {
    // 鍒涘缓瀹㈡埛绔?    client := agentos.NewClient(agentos.WithEndpoint("localhost:8080"))
    defer client.Close()

    // 鍒涘缓浠诲姟
    ctx := context.Background()
    task, err := client.Task.Submit(ctx, &agentos.SubmitRequest{
        Intent:    "鍒嗘瀽鏈搴︾殑閿€鍞暟鎹?,
        Priority:  1,
        TimeoutMs: 30000,
    })
    if err != nil {
        panic(err)
    }

    // 绛夊緟缁撴灉
    result, err := client.Task.Wait(ctx, task.Id, 30000)
    if err != nil {
        panic(err)
    }

    fmt.Printf("浠诲姟瀹屾垚: %s\n", result.Output)
}
```

#### 9.2.3 鏍稿績 API

**瀹㈡埛绔垵濮嬪寲**锛?```go
// 鍩虹閰嶇疆
client := agentos.NewClient()

// 甯﹁璇侀厤缃?client := agentos.NewClient(
    agentos.WithEndpoint("localhost:8080"),
    agentos.WithAPIKey("your-api-key"),
    agentos.WithTimeout(30*time.Second),
    agentos.WithMaxRetries(3),
)
```

**浠诲姟绠＄悊**锛?```go
// 鎻愪氦浠诲姟
task, err := client.Task.Submit(ctx, request)

// 绛夊緟浠诲姟
result, err := client.Task.Wait(ctx, taskId, timeoutMs)

// 鍙栨秷浠诲姟
err = client.Task.Cancel(ctx, taskId)

// 鏌ヨ鐘舵€?status, err := client.Task.Status(ctx, taskId)
```

**璁板繂绠＄悊**锛?```go
// 鍐欏叆璁板繂
err = client.Memory.Write(ctx, &agentos.MemoryWriteRequest{
    Content: "浠婂ぉ瀛︿範浜嗗井鍐呮牳鏋舵瀯",
    Tags:   []string{"瀛︿範", "鏋舵瀯"},
})

// 鎼滅储璁板繂
results, err := client.Memory.Search(ctx, &agentos.MemorySearchRequest{
    Query:  "寰唴鏍告灦鏋?,
    TopK:   10,
})
```

### 9.3 Python SDK

#### 9.3.1 瀹夎

```bash
pip install agentos-sdk
```

#### 9.3.2 蹇€熷紑濮?
```python
import asyncio
from agentos import AgentOSClient

async def main():
    # 鍒涘缓瀹㈡埛绔?    client = AgentOSClient(endpoint="localhost:8080")
    
    # 鎻愪氦浠诲姟
    task = await client.task.submit(
        intent="鍒嗘瀽閿€鍞暟鎹?,
        priority=1,
        timeout_ms=30000
    )
    
    # 绛夊緟缁撴灉
    result = await client.task.wait(task.id, timeout_ms=30000)
    print(f"浠诲姟瀹屾垚: {result.output}")

asyncio.run(main())
```

#### 9.3.3 鏍稿績 API

**鍚屾鐢ㄦ硶**锛?```python

client = AgentOSClient()

# 鍚屾璋冪敤

    intent="鍒嗘瀽閿€鍞暟鎹?,
    priority=1
)

```

**寮傛鐢ㄦ硶**锛?```python

from agentos import AsyncAgentOSClient

async def main():
    client = AsyncAgentOSClient()
    task = await client.task.submit(intent="鍒嗘瀽閿€鍞暟鎹?)
    result = await client.task.wait(task.id)
```

**璁板繂绠＄悊**锛?```python

await client.memory.write(
    content="浠婂ぉ瀛︿範浜嗗井鍐呮牳鏋舵瀯",
    tags=["瀛︿範", "鏋舵瀯"]

### 9.4 Rust SDK

#### 9.4.1 瀹夎

```toml
[dependencies]
agentos-sdk = "0.1"
tokio = { version = "1", features = ["full"] }
```

#### 9.4.2 蹇€熷紑濮?
```rust
use agentos_sdk::{Client, SubmitRequest};

#[tokio::main]
async fn main() -> Result<(), Box<dyn std::error::Error>> {
    // 鍒涘缓瀹㈡埛绔?    let client = Client::new("localhost:8080").await?;

    // 鎻愪氦浠诲姟
    let task = client
        .task()
        .submit(SubmitRequest {
            intent: "鍒嗘瀽閿€鍞暟鎹?.to_string(),
            priority: 1,
            timeout_ms: 30000,
        })
        .await?;

    // 绛夊緟缁撴灉
    let result = client.task().wait(&task.id, 30000).await?;

    println!("浠诲姟瀹屾垚: {}", result.output);
    Ok(())
}
```

#### 9.4.3 鏍稿績 API

```rust
// 瀹㈡埛绔厤缃?let client = Client::builder()
    .endpoint("localhost:8080")
    .api_key("your-api-key")
    .timeout(Duration::from_secs(30))
    .max_retries(3)
    .build()
    .await?;

// 浠诲姟绠＄悊
let task = client.task().submit(request).await?;
let result = client.task().wait(&task.id, 30000).await?;
client.task().cancel(&task.id).await?;

// 璁板繂绠＄悊
client.memory().write(write_request).await?;
let results = client.memory().search(search_request).await?;
```

### 10.3 鍩哄噯娴嬭瘯缁撴灉

#### 10.3.1 Syscall 鎬ц兘

**绌鸿浇 Syscall 寤惰繜**锛?
| 鎸囨爣 | 鏁板€?| 璇存槑 |
|------|------|------|
| **P50** | 3渭s | 涓綅鏁板欢杩?|
| **P95** | 5渭s | 95% 鍒嗕綅寤惰繜 |
| **P99** | 8渭s | 99% 鍒嗕綅寤惰繜 |

### 12.2 Docker 瀹瑰櫒鍖栭儴缃?
#### 12.2.1 Dockerfile 绀轰緥

```dockerfile
FROM ubuntu:24.04 AS builder

# 瀹夎渚濊禆
RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
    cmake gcc g++ make git curl

# 缂栬瘧 AgentOS
WORKDIR /build
COPY . .
RUN mkdir build && cd build && \
    cmake .. -DCMAKE_BUILD_TYPE=Release && \
    make -j$(nproc)

# 杩愯闀滃儚
FROM ubuntu:24.04
COPY --from=builder /build/build /opt/agentos
WORKDIR /opt/agentos
ENTRYPOINT ["./bin/agentos"]
```

#### 12.2.2 Docker Compose 閰嶇疆

```yaml
version: '3.8'
services:
  agentos:
    image: agentos:v1.0
    container_name: agentos_core
    ports:
      - "8080:8080"
    volumes:
      - ./data:/data
      - ./manager:/manager
    environment:
      - AGENTOS_MODE=production
    cpus: '4'
    mem_limit: 8g

  llm_d:
    image: agentos:v1.0
    container_name: agentos_llm
    command: bin/llm_d
    depends_on:
      - agentos

  monit_d:
    image: agentos:v1.0
    container_name: agentos_monit
    command: bin/monit_d
    depends_on:
      - agentos
```

### 12.3 Kubernetes 閮ㄧ讲

#### 12.3.1 Deployment 绀轰緥

```yaml
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
metadata:
  name: agentos-core
spec:
  replicas: 3
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app: agentos-core
  template:
    metadata:
      labels:
        app: agentos-core
    spec:
      containers:
      - name: agentos
        image: agentos:v1.0
        ports:
        - containerPort: 8080
        resources:
          requests:
            memory: "2Gi"
            cpu: "2"
          limits:
            memory: "8Gi"
            cpu: "4"
        livenessProbe:
          httpGet:
            path: /health
            port: 8080
          initialDelaySeconds: 30
        readinessProbe:
          httpGet:
            path: /ready
            port: 8080
          initialDelaySeconds: 10
```

#### 12.3.2 Service 绀轰緥

```yaml
apiVersion: v1
kind: Service
metadata:
  name: agentos-service
spec:
  selector:
    app: agentos-core
  ports:
  - protocol: TCP
    port: 80
    targetPort: 8080
  type: LoadBalancer
```

### 14.2 鎻掍欢寮€鍙戞寚鍗?
#### 14.2.1 鎻掍欢鎺ュ彛

```c
/**
 * @brief AgentOS 鎻掍欢鎺ュ彛
 */
typedef struct agentos_plugin {
    const char* name;                    // 鎻掍欢鍚嶇О
    const char* version;                  // 鎻掍欢鐗堟湰
    agentos_error_t (*init)(void);       // 鍒濆鍖?    agentos_error_t (*shutdown)(void);    // 娓呯悊
    agentos_error_t (*on_task)(task_t*); // 浠诲姟閽╁瓙
} agentos_plugin_t;
```

#### 14.2.2 鎻掍欢绀轰緥

```go
package main

type MyPlugin struct{}

func (p *MyPlugin) Name() string { return "my-plugin" }
func (p *MyPlugin) Version() string { return "1.0.0" }

func (p *MyPlugin) OnTask(task *Task) error {
    // 澶勭悊浠诲姟
    return nil
}

plugin.Register(&MyPlugin{})
```
